---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> In this first half of\
  \ this lecture, Professor Zhao shows how to prove Szemer\xE9di&rsquo;s theorem using\
  \ the hypergraph removal lemma, as well as a discussion of the hypergraph regularity\
  \ method.</p><p>In the second half, he discusses a spectral graph theoretic proof\
  \ of Szemer\xE9di&rsquo;s regularity lemma.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>\
  \ Yufei Zhao</p>"
course_id: 18-217-graph-theory-and-additive-combinatorics-fall-2019

  <span m="1690280">important</span> <span m="1690670">concept</span> <span m="1691480">in</span>
  <span m="1692350">mathematics</span> <span m="1692920">and</span> <span m="1693010">computer</span>
  <span m="1693310">science,</span> <span m="1693640">and</span> <span m="1694000">it's</span>
  <span m="1694150">a</span> <span m="1694180">very</span> <span m="1694390">important</span>
  <span m="1694810">idea.</span></p><p><span m="1696300">But</span> <span m="1696340">of</span>
  <span m="1696430">course,</span> <span m="1696670">you</span> <span m="1696760">can</span>
  <span m="1696970">generate</span> <span m="1697480">a</span> <span m="1697540">pseudo</span>
  <span m="1697870">random</span> <span m="1698170">object</span> <span m="1698530">by</span>
  <span m="1698650">just</span> <span m="1698830">taking</span> <span m="1699100">a</span>
  <span m="1699160">random</span> <span m="1699550">object,</span> <span m="1700510">and</span>
  <span m="1701140">it</span> <span m="1701530">should</span> <span m="1701830">hopefully</span>
  <span m="1702220">satisfy</span> <span m="1702730">some</span> <span m="1702910">properties</span>
  <span m="1703360">of</span> <span m="1703450">pseudo</span> <span m="1703720">randomness.</span>
  <span m="1704560">So</span> <span m="1704680">let's</span> <span m="1704860">see</span>
  <span m="1706090">what</span> <span m="1707410">this</span> <span m="1707770">notion</span>
  <span m="1709000">of</span> <span m="1709600">regularity,</span> <span m="1710900">how</span>
  <span m="1711180">it</span> <span m="1711310">works</span> <span m="1711700">even</span>
  <span m="1711970">for</span> <span m="1712390">random</span> <span m="1713380">hypergraph.</span>
  <span m="1716030">What's</span> <span m="1716270">a</span> <span m="1716300">random</span>
  <span m="1716690">hypergraph?</span> <span m="1718280">So</span> <span m="1718430">there</span>
  <span m="1718580">are</span> <span m="1719060">different</span> <span m="1719390">ways</span>
  <span m="1719690">to</span> <span m="1719780">generate</span> <span m="1720290">a</span>
  <span m="1720350">random</span> <span m="1720740">hypergraph.</span> <span m="1722830">One</span>
  <span m="1723100">way</span> <span m="1723490">is</span> <span m="1723700">to</span>
  <span m="1724420">have</span> <span m="1726350">a</span> <span m="1726440">bunch</span>
  <span m="1726710">of</span> <span m="1726860">triples</span> <span m="1727640">all</span>
  <span m="1727820">appearing</span> <span m="1728600">uniformly</span> <span m="1729290">at</span>
  <span m="1729410">random,</span> <span m="1730130">independently</span> <span m="1730790">at</span>
  <span m="1730940">random.</span></p><p><span m="1733630">So</span> <span m="1733740">I</span>
  <span m="1733830">have</span> <span m="1734610">a</span> <span m="1734700">bunch</span>
  <span m="1734910">of</span> <span m="1735060">possible</span> <span m="1735480">triples</span>
  <span m="1735810">that</span> <span m="1735900">I</span> <span m="1735960">can</span>
  <span m="1736020">make</span> <span m="1736200">as</span> <span m="1736440">edges,</span>
  <span m="1736860">each</span> <span m="1737040">one</span> <span m="1737270">I</span>
  <span m="1737340">flip</span> <span m="1737580">a</span> <span m="1737640">coin.</span>
  <span m="1739210">But</span> <span m="1739360">there's</span> <span m="1739510">a</span>
  <span m="1739570">different</span> <span m="1739810">way,</span> <span m="1740260">and</span>
  <span m="1740350">let</span> <span m="1740440">me</span> <span m="1741010">show</span>
  <span m="1741190">you</span> <span m="1741310">a</span> <span m="1741370">different</span>
  <span m="1741640">way</span> <span m="1741760">to</span> <span m="1741880">generate</span>
  <span m="1742330">a</span> <span m="1742420">random</span> <span m="1743260">three</span>
  <span m="1743470">graph.</span> <span m="1751080">Let</span> <span m="1751170">me</span>
  <span m="1751290">give</span> <span m="1751470">you</span> <span m="1751590">two</span>
  <span m="1751800">parameters,</span> <span m="1753870">p</span> <span m="1754260">and</span>
  <span m="1754410">q.</span> <span m="1755480">They</span> <span m="1755700">are</span>
  <span m="1755940">constants</span> <span m="1756570">between</span> <span m="1756930">0</span>
  <span m="1757290">and</span> <span m="1757440">1.</span> <span m="1763630">So</span>
  <span m="1763770">let's</span> <span m="1764130">build</span> <span m="1765120">first</span>
  <span m="1766470">a</span> <span m="1767370">graph,</span> <span m="1768930">so</span>
  <span m="1769035">a</span> <span m="1769140">random</span> <span m="1769620">two</span>
  <span m="1769860">graph</span> <span m="1774370">which</span> <span m="1774520">I'll</span>
  <span m="1774670">call</span> <span m="1776250">g2.</span> <span m="1777630">So</span>
  <span m="1777780">this</span> <span m="1778020">is</span> <span m="1778260">just</span>
  <span m="1778890">the</span> <span m="1779040">Erdos-Renyi</span> <span m="1779910">random</span>
  <span m="1780300">graph,</span> <span m="1780630">gnp.</span> <span m="1781560">The</span>
  <span m="1781680">usual</span> <span m="1782040">one</span> <span m="1782340">where</span>
  <span m="1782640">you</span> <span m="1782820">flip</span> <span m="1783540">a</span>
  <span m="1783600">coin</span> <span m="1783930">for</span> <span m="1784110">each</span>
  <span m="1784350">edge</span> <span m="1784900">so</span> <span m="1785040">that</span>
  <span m="1785220">each</span> <span m="1785430">edge</span> <span m="1785640">appears</span>
  <span m="1786030">with</span> <span m="1786180">probability</span> <span m="1786720">p</span>
  <span m="1787440">independently.</span></p><p><span m="1790000">And</span> <span

  <span m="1793870">the</span> <span m="1794020">actual</span> <span m="1794740">three</span>
  <span m="1794980">graph</span> <span m="1795220">that</span> <span m="1795390">want,</span>
  <span m="1795940">g3,</span> <span m="1796900">by</span> <span m="1798400">including</span>
  <span m="1802820">every</span> <span m="1803120">triple,</span> <span m="1805530">so</span>
  <span m="1805740">every</span> <span m="1808920">triangle</span> <span m="1813540">of</span>
  <span m="1813870">g</span> <span m="1817550">has</span> <span m="1817850">an</span>
  <span m="1818120">edge.</span> <span m="1819260">So</span> <span m="1819330">here,</span>

  <span m="1830880">So</span> <span m="1831000">it's</span> <span m="1831090">a</span>

  <span m="1839070">triple</span> <span m="1839740">with</span> <span m="1839950">a</span>
  <span m="1840180">probability</span> <span m="1841203">q.</span> <span m="1842050">If</span>
  <span m="1842170">you</span> <span m="1842270">like,</span> <span m="1842530">q</span>
  <span m="1842890">be</span> <span m="1843010">even</span> <span m="1843280">one.</span>
  <span m="1843790">So</span> <span m="1844060">I</span> <span m="1844960">do</span>
  <span m="1845100">a</span> <span m="1845170">random</span> <span m="1845470">graph</span>

  <span m="1915040">q.</span></p><p><span m="1918530">So</span> <span m="1918920">they</span>
  <span m="1919070">have</span> <span m="1919310">similar</span> <span m="1919740">edge</span>

  <span m="1923390">you</span> <span m="1923480">can</span> <span m="1923690">check</span>

  <span m="1946610">high</span> <span m="1946790">probability.</span> <span m="1951360">OK.</span>
  <span m="1952110">Great.</span> <span m="1953470">So</span> <span m="1954700">if</span>
  <span m="1954970">you</span> <span m="1955120">have</span> <span m="1955290">the</span>

  <span m="1967830">they</span> <span m="1967980">the</span> <span m="1968070">same?</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1989400">the</span> <span m="1989450">second</span> <span m="1989750">case</span>
  <span m="1989990">first.</span> <span m="1990980">In</span> <span m="1991100">b,</span>
  <span m="1992120">so</span> <span m="1993050">what's</span> <span m="1993320">the</span>

  <span m="1995750">have</span> <span m="1996050">four</span> <span m="1996500">vertices,</span>

  <span m="2012400">What</span> <span m="2012530">about</span> <span m="2012660">the</span>
  <span m="2012750">first</span> <span m="2012930">one?</span></p><p><span m="2015930">AUDIENCE:</span>
  <span m="2016405">6.</span></p><p><span m="2018310">PROFESSOR:</span> <span m="2018485">So</span>
  <span m="2018660">in</span> <span m="2018690">the</span> <span m="2018720">first</span>
  <span m="2019020">one,</span> <span m="2020280">to</span> <span m="2020490">get</span>

  <span m="2021990">underlying</span> <span m="2022590">graph</span> <span m="2023130">needs</span>
  <span m="2023400">to</span> <span m="2023490">have</span> <span m="2023640">a</span>
  <span m="2023670">k4.</span> <span m="2025230">So</span> <span m="2025470">p</span>

  <span m="2027840">and</span> <span m="2027960">then</span> <span m="2028140">on</span>

  <span m="2028830">I</span> <span m="2028920">want</span> <span m="2029310">4q's.</span>
  <span m="2031720">So</span> <span m="2031920">p</span> <span m="2032130">raised</span>
  <span m="2032370">to</span> <span m="2032430">6,</span> <span m="2032610">q</span>
  <span m="2032990">raise</span> <span m="2033210">to</span> <span m="2033300">4.</span>
  <span m="2034170">And</span> <span m="2034320">when</span> <span m="2034500">p</span>
  <span m="2034800">is</span> <span m="2034920">different,</span> <span m="2035220">these</span>
  <span m="2035400">numbers</span> <span m="2035790">are</span> <span m="2035880">different.</span>
  <span m="2039500">So</span> <span m="2039550">this</span> <span m="2039760">is</span>
  <span m="2040300">an</span> <span m="2040420">example</span> <span m="2040840">showing</span>

  <span m="2045250">two</span> <span m="2045490">different</span> <span m="2045790">graphs</span>

  <span m="2048699">but</span> <span m="2048850">have</span> <span m="2049030">vastly</span>
  <span m="2049480">different</span> <span m="2050290">densities</span> <span m="2050830">of</span>
  <span m="2050949">tetrahedra.</span> <span m="2055600">Any</span> <span m="2055750">questions</span>
  <span m="2056170">about</span> <span m="2056350">this</span> <span m="2056530">example?</span></p><p><span
  m="2060429">It</span> <span m="2060579">shows</span> <span m="2060730">you,</span>
  <span m="2061460">at</span> <span m="2061710">least,</span> <span m="2062380">why</span>
  <span m="2062739">this</span> <span m="2063040">naive</span> <span m="2063460">attempt</span>
  <span m="2064330">does</span> <span m="2064540">not</span> <span m="2064870">work,</span>
  <span m="2066132">at</span> <span m="2066351">least</span> <span m="2066570">if</span>
  <span m="2066670">you</span> <span m="2066800">follow</span> <span m="2067159">our</span>
  <span m="2067699">regularity</span> <span m="2068300">recipe.</span> <span m="2074730">But</span>
  <span m="2074920">in</span> <span m="2075080">any</span> <span m="2075239">case,</span>
  <span m="2075739">it's</span> <span m="2076650">good</span> <span m="2076830">for</span>
  <span m="2077010">something.</span> <span m="2077500">So</span> <span m="2078469">you</span>
  <span m="2078659">do</span> <span m="2078739">not</span> <span m="2078870">have</span>
  <span m="2079030">a</span> <span m="2079530">counting</span> <span m="2079800">lemma</span>
  <span m="2080010">for</span> <span m="2080130">tetrahedra,</span> <span m="2081010">but</span>
  <span m="2082600">you</span> <span m="2083130">can</span> <span m="2083340">still</span>
  <span m="2083639">salvage</span> <span m="2084060">something.</span> <span m="2084690">So</span>
  <span m="2085830">it</span> <span m="2085920">turns</span> <span m="2086219">out</span>
  <span m="2087810">there</span> <span m="2088020">is</span> <span m="2088199">a</span>
  <span m="2088280">counting</span> <span m="2088610">lemma</span> <span m="2091600">if</span>
  <span m="2091780">your</span> <span m="2091929">graph</span> <span m="2092320">h--</span>
  <span m="2100820">if</span> <span m="2101110">this</span> <span m="2101340">r</span>
  <span m="2101530">graph</span> <span m="2101870">h</span> <span m="2102140">is</span>
  <span m="2102330">linear.</span> <span m="2104640">So</span> <span m="2104850">linear</span>
  <span m="2105240">means</span> <span m="2105960">every</span> <span m="2106920">pair</span>
  <span m="2107220">of</span> <span m="2107400">edges</span> <span m="2107760">intersecting</span>
  <span m="2108390">at</span> <span m="2108450">most</span> <span m="2108690">one</span>
  <span m="2108900">vertex.</span></p><p><span m="2122700">So</span> <span m="2122780">for</span>
  <span m="2122960">example,</span> <span m="2126560">if</span> <span m="2126640">you</span>
  <span m="2126730">look</span> <span m="2126970">at--</span> <span m="2132640">so</span>
  <span m="2133660">hypergraph</span> <span m="2133930">or</span> <span m="2134290">each</span>
  <span m="2134590">line</span> <span m="2134920">is</span> <span m="2135100">an</span>
  <span m="2135220">edge</span> <span m="2135520">of</span> <span m="2135610">triples.</span>
  <span m="2136930">So</span> <span m="2137050">that's</span> <span m="2137410">a</span>
  <span m="2137470">linear</span> <span m="2137770">hypergraph</span> <span m="2138045">because</span>
  <span m="2138550">each</span> <span m="2138850">pair</span> <span m="2139480">intersecting</span>
  <span m="2140050">at</span> <span m="2140110">most</span> <span m="2140380">one</span>
  <span m="2140560">vertex.</span> <span m="2141700">Tetrahedron</span> <span m="2142340">is</span>
  <span m="2142480">not</span> <span m="2142720">linear.</span> <span m="2143440">Two</span>
  <span m="2143620">faces</span> <span m="2144010">of</span> <span m="2144100">a</span>
  <span m="2144340">tetrahedron</span> <span m="2144615">can</span> <span m="2144890">intersect</span>

  <span m="2147526">OK.</span> <span m="2148000">So</span> <span m="2148100">we</span>

  <span m="2149980">actually,</span> <span m="2150250">the</span> <span m="2150310">proof</span>

  <span m="2153100">we</span> <span m="2153220">saw</span> <span m="2153460">for</span>
  <span m="2153610">graphs.</span> <span m="2156730">Yes.</span></p><p><span m="2157325">AUDIENCE:</span>

  <span m="2561660">triangles,</span> <span m="2562910">and</span> <span m="2562980">that's</span>

  <span m="2914820">great.</span> <span m="2916860">But</span> <span m="2917070">there</span>
  <span m="2917280">are</span> <span m="2917340">better</span> <span m="2917610">proofs.</span>
  <span m="2918310">So</span> <span m="2918950">there</span> <span m="2919320">are</span>
  <span m="2919500">more</span> <span m="2919680">efficient</span> <span m="2920070">proofs</span>

  <span m="3224850">a</span> <span m="3225120">graph</span> <span m="3225450">to</span>
  <span m="3225570">this</span> <span m="3225750">matrix.</span></p><p><span m="3226640">So</span>
  <span m="3228480">this</span> <span m="3228660">graph</span> <span m="3228930">here</span>
  <span m="3229260">would</span> <span m="3229570">be</span> <span m="3231950">like</span>
  <span m="3232450">that</span> <span m="3233450">and</span> <span m="3233700">so</span>
  <span m="3233950">on.</span> <span m="3236670">It's</span> <span m="3236880">a</span>
  <span m="3237120">real</span> <span m="3237510">symmetric</span> <span m="3237990">matrix</span>
  <span m="3242030">and</span> <span m="3242200">that's</span> <span m="3242410">always</span>
  <span m="3243290">pretty</span> <span m="3243550">nice.</span> <span m="3244360">Symmetric</span>
  <span m="3245170">matrices</span> <span m="3245710">have</span> <span m="3245920">lots</span>
  <span m="3246190">of</span> <span m="3246310">great</span> <span m="3246550">properties</span>
  <span m="3247870">that</span> <span m="3248050">will</span> <span m="3248170">be</span>
  <span m="3248290">convenient</span> <span m="3248740">to</span> <span m="3248830">use.</span>
  <span m="3249200">In</span> <span m="3249300">fact,</span> <span m="3250360">if</span>
  <span m="3250460">you're</span> <span m="3250560">like</span> <span m="3250630">myself,</span>
  <span m="3251050">if</span> <span m="3251170">you're</span> <span m="3251290">too</span>
  <span m="3251500">used</span> <span m="3251740">to</span> <span m="3251890">working</span>

  <span m="3255700">general</span> <span m="3256330">to</span> <span m="3256720">non-symmetric</span>
  <span m="3257380">matrices.</span> <span m="3258460">But</span> <span m="3259540">it</span>

  <span m="3260560">we're</span> <span m="3260680">happy.</span> <span m="3261440">So</span>
  <span m="3262090">for</span> <span m="3262270">symmetric</span> <span m="3262660">matrices,</span>

  <span m="3264160">set</span> <span m="3264400">of</span> <span m="3264490">real</span>

  <span m="4018490">this</span> <span m="4018670">notion</span> <span m="4019120">of</span>
  <span m="4019390">a</span> <span m="4020260">spectral</span> <span m="4020800">radius</span>
  <span m="4024890">or</span> <span m="4025050">sometimes</span> <span m="4025440">called</span>
  <span m="4025590">spectral</span> <span m="4026040">norm.</span></p><p><span m="4029200">So</span>
  <span m="4029500">far</span> <span m="4029770">I'm</span> <span m="4029950">only</span>
  <span m="4030190">going</span> <span m="4030400">to</span> <span m="4030640">discuss</span>
  <span m="4031450">real</span> <span m="4031750">symmetric</span> <span m="4032230">matrices.</span>
  <span m="4033160">So</span> <span m="4033640">many</span> <span m="4033910">of</span>
  <span m="4034000">the</span> <span m="4034060">things</span> <span m="4034330">I</span>
  <span m="4034390">will</span> <span m="4034480">say</span> <span m="4034750">are</span>
  <span m="4034870">not</span> <span m="4035200">true</span> <span m="4035470">for</span>
  <span m="4036220">if</span> <span m="4036340">you're</span> <span m="4036460">not</span>
  <span m="4036670">in</span> <span m="4036760">a</span> <span m="4036820">real</span>
  <span m="4037060">symmetric</span> <span m="4037450">case.</span> <span m="4038110">So</span>
  <span m="4038290">the</span> <span m="4038380">spectral</span> <span m="4038830">radius</span>
  <span m="4039130">spectral</span> <span m="4039490">norm</span> <span m="4043230">of</span>
  <span m="4043490">a</span> <span m="4045200">is</span> <span m="4045680">the</span>
  <span m="4046220">largest</span> <span m="4050220">eigenvalue</span> <span m="4051030">of</span>

  <span m="4079010">out</span> <span m="4079100">to</span> <span m="4079190">be</span>
  <span m="4079310">a</span> <span m="4079340">max,</span> <span m="4080120">of</span>
